SELECT 
	                     tools.Tool_ID,tools.Employee_ID,tools.Building_ID,tools.Description,tools.Size,tools.Brand,tools.SerialNumber,tools.Calibration_Frequency,tools.IsEnabled,tools.IsEclipseTool,tools.Status , lt1.Dep_ID,
                        IF(lt1.Employee_ID = 0, 'Eclipse Automation', CONCAT(lt1.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt1.Employee_Last_Name)) AS Employee_Name, 
                        build.Address AS Building_Address, 
                         records.Record_ID,records.Tool_ID,records.Employee_ID,records.Calibration_Date,records.Master_Used,records.Acceptable_Tolerance,if (records.Passed is null OR records.Passed = false, 'false', 'true') as Passed,if (records.IsVoid is null OR records.IsVoid = false, 'false', 'true') as IsVoid,records.FileName ,
                        CONCAT(lt2.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt2.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name,
	                    CONCAT((SELECT FullPath FROM pathdata WHERE `name` = 'Tools_CalibrationRecords'), records.FileName) AS FilePath,
	                     readings.Reading_ID,readings.Record_ID,readings.ReadingAt,readings.ReadingFound,readings.ReadingLeft ,
                         stat.Status_ID,stat.Status_Description ,
                         notes.Note_ID,notes.Tool_ID,notes.Employee_ID,notes.Note_Type,notes.Note_Reason,notes.Note_Date ,
                        CONCAT(lt3.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt3.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name
                    FROM
	                    tools
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationrecords records on tools.Tool_ID = records.Tool_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationreadings readings on records.Record_ID = readings.Record_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    buildings build on tools.Building_ID = build.ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt1 on tools.Employee_ID = lt1.Employee_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt2 on records.Employee_ID = lt2.Employee_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_status stat on tools.Status = stat.Status_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_notes notes on tools.Tool_ID = notes.Tool_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt3 on notes.Employee_ID = lt3.Employee_ID
                    
                    ORDER BY
	                    tools.Tool_ID, records.Record_ID desc, readings.Reading_ID, notes.Note_Date desc;

SELECT 
                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

SELECT 
                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

SELECT 
                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

SELECT 
                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

                     parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
                    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,
                    t.Ass_ID,
                    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
                    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),
                            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
                    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
                FROM
                    parts
                        JOIN
                    manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
                        LEFT JOIN
                    (SELECT 
                        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
                    FROM
                        assemblies_b b
                    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
                    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
                        LEFT JOIN
                    parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
		                LEFT JOIN
	                (SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
                WHERE
                    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
                ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

SELECT 
    parts.ID,parts.CATALOG_NO,parts.DESCRIPTION,parts.DESCRIPTIONHG,parts.ACADDESCR,parts.MANUFACT_TAG,parts.TEMPLATE,parts.COST,parts.COST_SCHED,parts.FOOT_PRINT_X,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Y,parts.FOOT_PRINT_Z,parts.DEVICE_CODE,parts.ABACOS_CODE,parts.USER_FIELD_1,parts.USER_FIELD_2,parts.USER_FIELD_3,parts.USER_FIELD_4,parts.EM,parts.NO_IN_STOCK,parts.BLOCK_NAME,parts.ALT_CATALOG_NO,parts.NO_CONTACTS,parts.NC_CONTACTS,parts.DISTRIBUTOR,parts.LEAD_TIME,parts.LEAD_UNIT,parts.SWTEMPLATE,parts.Dummy_ID,parts.DataSheet,parts.Notes,parts.COST_SE,parts.COST_SCHED_SE,parts.COST_AZ,parts.COST_SCHED_AZ,parts.COST_SW,parts.COST_SCHED_SW,parts.COST_DD,parts.COST_SCHED_DD,parts.COST_HG,parts.COST_SCHED_HG,parts.COST_EI,parts.COST_SCHED_EI,parts.COST_MY,parts.COST_SCHED_MY,parts.COST_DE,parts.COST_SCHED_DE,parts.COST_CH,parts.COST_SCHED_CH,parts.ForeignFunds,parts.Currency_ID,parts.ForeignFundsSE,parts.Currency_IDSE,parts.ForeignFundsSW,parts.Currency_IDSW,parts.ForeignFundsAZ,parts.Currency_IDAZ,parts.ForeignFundsDD,parts.Currency_IDDD,parts.ForeignFundsHG,parts.Currency_IDHG,parts.ForeignFundsEI,parts.Currency_IDEI,parts.ForeignFundsMY,parts.Currency_IDMY,parts.ForeignFundsDE,parts.Currency_IDDE,parts.ForeignFundsCH,parts.Currency_IDCH,parts.Obsolete,parts.HS_Code,parts.Country_Of_Origin ,
    manufacturers.MFG_NAME,    t.Ass_ID,    t.PART_NO_IN_ASSY,
    CONCAT(COALESCE(p2.MANUFACT_TAG, parts.MANUFACT_TAG),            COALESCE(t.First_Part_ID, parts.ID)) AS SortString,
    inv.NO_IN_STOCK
FROM
    parts
	JOIN 
		manufacturers ON parts.MANUFACT_TAG = manufacturers.MFG_TAG
    LEFT JOIN
	    (SELECT 
	        Ass_ID, Part_ID, a.First_Part_ID, PART_NO_IN_ASSY
	    FROM
	        assemblies_b b
	    LEFT JOIN assemblies_a a ON b.ASS_ID = a.ID
	    GROUP BY Ass_ID , Part_ID
		) t ON t.Part_ID = parts.ID
	LEFT JOIN 
		parts p2 ON p2.ID = t.First_Part_ID
    LEFT JOIN
    	(SELECT Part_ID, SUM(NO_IN_STOCK) AS NO_IN_STOCK from partsinventory group by Part_ID) inv ON inv.Part_ID = parts.ID
WHERE
    manufacturers.Obsolete = 0
ORDER BY MFG_NAME;

	                     readings.Reading_ID,readings.Record_ID,readings.ReadingAt,readings.ReadingFound,readings.ReadingLeft ,
                         stat.Status_ID,stat.Status_Description ,
                         notes.Note_ID,notes.Tool_ID,notes.Employee_ID,notes.Note_Type,notes.Note_Reason,notes.Note_Date ,
                        CONCAT(lt3.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt3.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name
                    FROM
	                    tools
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationrecords records on tools.Tool_ID = records.Tool_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationreadings readings on records.Record_ID = readings.Record_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    buildings build on tools.Building_ID = build.ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt1 on tools.Employee_ID = lt1.Employee_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt2 on records.Employee_ID = lt2.Employee_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_status stat on tools.Status = stat.Status_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_notes notes on tools.Tool_ID = notes.Tool_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt3 on notes.Employee_ID = lt3.Employee_ID
                    
                    ORDER BY
	                    tools.Tool_ID, records.Record_ID desc, readings.Reading_ID, notes.Note_Date desc;

SELECT 
	                     tools.Tool_ID,tools.Employee_ID,tools.Building_ID,tools.Description,tools.Size,tools.Brand,tools.SerialNumber,tools.Calibration_Frequency,tools.IsEnabled,tools.IsEclipseTool,tools.Status , lt1.Dep_ID,
                        IF(lt1.Employee_ID = 0, 'Eclipse Automation', CONCAT(lt1.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt1.Employee_Last_Name)) AS Employee_Name, 
                        build.Address AS Building_Address, 
                         records.Record_ID,records.Tool_ID,records.Employee_ID,records.Calibration_Date,records.Master_Used,records.Acceptable_Tolerance,if (records.Passed is null OR records.Passed = false, 'false', 'true') as Passed,if (records.IsVoid is null OR records.IsVoid = false, 'false', 'true') as IsVoid,records.FileName ,
                        CONCAT(lt2.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt2.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name,
	                    CONCAT((SELECT FullPath FROM pathdata WHERE `name` = 'Tools_CalibrationRecords'), records.FileName) AS FilePath,
	                     readings.Reading_ID,readings.Record_ID,readings.ReadingAt,readings.ReadingFound,readings.ReadingLeft ,
                         stat.Status_ID,stat.Status_Description ,
                         notes.Note_ID,notes.Tool_ID,notes.Employee_ID,notes.Note_Type,notes.Note_Reason,notes.Note_Date ,
                        CONCAT(lt3.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt3.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name
                    FROM
	                    tools
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationrecords records on tools.Tool_ID = records.Tool_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationreadings readings on records.Record_ID = readings.Record_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    buildings build on tools.Building_ID = build.ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt1 on tools.Employee_ID = lt1.Employee_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt2 on records.Employee_ID = lt2.Employee_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_status stat on tools.Status = stat.Status_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_notes notes on tools.Tool_ID = notes.Tool_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt3 on notes.Employee_ID = lt3.Employee_ID
                    
                    ORDER BY
	                    tools.Tool_ID, records.Record_ID desc, readings.Reading_ID, notes.Note_Date desc;

SELECT 
	                     tools.Tool_ID,tools.Employee_ID,tools.Building_ID,tools.Description,tools.Size,tools.Brand,tools.SerialNumber,tools.Calibration_Frequency,tools.IsEnabled,tools.IsEclipseTool,tools.Status , lt1.Dep_ID,
                        IF(lt1.Employee_ID = 0, 'Eclipse Automation', CONCAT(lt1.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt1.Employee_Last_Name)) AS Employee_Name, 
                        build.Address AS Building_Address, 
                         records.Record_ID,records.Tool_ID,records.Employee_ID,records.Calibration_Date,records.Master_Used,records.Acceptable_Tolerance,if (records.Passed is null OR records.Passed = false, 'false', 'true') as Passed,if (records.IsVoid is null OR records.IsVoid = false, 'false', 'true') as IsVoid,records.FileName ,
                        CONCAT(lt2.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt2.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name,
	                    CONCAT((SELECT FullPath FROM pathdata WHERE `name` = 'Tools_CalibrationRecords'), records.FileName) AS FilePath,
	                     readings.Reading_ID,readings.Record_ID,readings.ReadingAt,readings.ReadingFound,readings.ReadingLeft ,
                         stat.Status_ID,stat.Status_Description ,
                         notes.Note_ID,notes.Tool_ID,notes.Employee_ID,notes.Note_Type,notes.Note_Reason,notes.Note_Date ,
                        CONCAT(lt3.Employee_First_Name, ' ', lt3.Employee_Last_Name) AS Employee_Name
                    FROM
	                    tools
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationrecords records on tools.Tool_ID = records.Tool_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    tools_calibrationreadings readings on records.Record_ID = readings.Record_ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    buildings build on tools.Building_ID = build.ID
		                    LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt1 on tools.Employee_ID = lt1.Employee_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt2 on records.Employee_ID = lt2.Employee_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_status stat on tools.Status = stat.Status_ID
                            LEFT JOIN
                        tools_notes notes on tools.Tool_ID = notes.Tool_ID
    		                LEFT JOIN
	                    login_table lt3 on notes.Employee_ID = lt3.Employee_ID
                    
                    ORDER BY
	                    tools.Tool_ID, records.Record_ID desc, readings.Reading_ID, notes.Note_Date desc;
